# Installation | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> In this article, we will cover installing Severe, and the most common issues users face in the process.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#requirements)

Requirements


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Windows 10/11:** Note that for some newer versions of **Windows 11** might not work, you should verify in the purchase channel on the Discord server. We also don't promise tweaked re-distributions of Windows to work out of the box, few that have been tested are: **Atlas**, and **XOS**.
    
*   **Internet Connection**
    
*   **Turned off anti-virus:** both Windows Defender, and user-installed anti-viruses can interfere with **Severe**. We recommend using [**Winaero Tweaker**](https://winaerotweaker.com/)
     or \[**Defender Control**\]\[https://github.com/pgkt04/defender-control\]
    

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#redistributes)

Redistributes

This is needed to be installed **before** Severe for smoother experience, and also to fix some of the problems (for example: the overlay not showing up).

*   [DirectX End-User Runtime](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=8109)
    
*   [.NET SDK](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/en-us/download)
    
*   [Visual C++ Runtime](https://www.techpowerup.com/download/visual-c-redistributable-runtime-package-all-in-one/)
    

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#downloading)

Downloading


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Install **severe.rar** from the `#downloads` channel on the official Discord server, afterwards continue by **extracting**, and **running the upgrade.exe** file.

After, you should see a new file in the same folder as **upgrade.exe** called **software.exe**, this is your primary executable that **you should be running to launch Severe.**

Run **software.exe**, and ideally, after a bit of waiting, you should see an overlay on **Roblox** asking you to either **log-in** or **register**. If you're a first time user, please continue with registering, a few key details however:

*   **Note down your username and password:** this is critical to ensure that your account won't get lost.
    
*   **Avoid special characters:** spaces, symbols should be avoided at all cost, please use an alphanumeric password consisting of letters **A-Z**, and **0-9** numbers.
    

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#issues)

Issues


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#hwid-mismatch)

HWID Mismatch

We utilize **HWID** to provide a secure connection from your machine to our servers, changing a part in your PC can sometimes cause this to change. In this case, please navigate to our [Keyauth Page](https://keyauth.cc/panel/SHELUV_PERKS/v-severe)
 and press **"Reset HWID"**.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#executable-not-opening)

Executable not opening

This is a frequent issue with custom file explorers, please use the native file explorer or utilize the command prompt to open the file.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#loading-loop-bad-post-code)

Loading Loop / Bad Post Code

Incase **Severe** is stuck whilst loading, the most frequent resolution is disabling your anti-virus software, such as **Malwarebytes**, or **Avast**.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#glfw-error)

GLFW Error

Reopen **Severe** with **Roblox window focused**.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#d3dcompiler_43.dll)

D3DCompiler\_43.dll

Download this [file](https://www.dll-files.com/download/0c20f567e2e586f6bcf3f0ce3ae64aab/d3dcompiler_43.dll.html?c=Yko1VjlUSWd4WFJaZ2w5OG1hQjFVQT09)
 and move it into `C:/Windows/System32`.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#https-verification-failed)

HTTPs Verification Failed

Use [**Cloudflare's 1.1.1.1**](https://one.one.one.one/)
 or a VPN.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#this-app-cant-run-on-your-pc)

This app can't run on your PC

Disable all anti-viruses, redownload **Severe** and run **upgrade.exe**.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#hosts)

Hosts

First, download [this file](https://pixeldrain.com/u/jWJfBB3Q)
, afterwards, move it to `C:/Windows/System32/Drivers/etc`.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation#dont-see-your-issue)

Don't see your issue?

Contact support via the official **Discord server**, and please, remain patient. In edge cases, where a new-user can't get their **Severe** working, and hasn't registered an account before, a refund can be negotiated.

[PreviousLanding](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing)
[NextGlossary](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/glossary)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Glossary | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/glossary.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/glossary#luau)

[Luau](https://luau.org/)



--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

(pronounced "LOO-ow") is a scripting language, derived from **Lua 5.1**, key features of it are **performance**, **type checking**, **syntax additions**, and **safety**.

It's used in **Roblox** as the primary scripting language for games, as well as in **Warframe**, and **Alan Wake 2**.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/glossary#hwid)

[HWID](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Device_fingerprint)



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Often used for authentication, it's a unique identifier assigned to hardware components of a computer.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/glossary#ram)

[RAM](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Random-access_memory)



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Digital, "short-term memory" in which games store live data, such as player health, position, etc.

[PreviousInstallation](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/installation)
[NextCore](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core)

# Miscellaneous | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#isrbxactive)

isrbxactive


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function isrbxactive(): boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#returns)

Returns

Copy

    boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description)

Description

Will return `true` if the currently focused window is **Roblox**, otherwise returns `false`.

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#send_notification)

send\_notification


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition-1)

Definition

Copy

    function send_notification(content: string): ()

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

content

string

Message, that you want to be visualized on the overlay.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-1)

Description

This will visualize `content` on the screen thru an notification on the overlay.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    send_notification 'Hello, world!'

* * *

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

content

string

Whatever you want to be copied into the clipboard.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-2)

Description

This will essentially copy the string to your system's clipboard.

###

Code Samples

Copy

    setclipboard 'Clipboard!'

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#block_roblox_window)

block\_roblox\_window


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition-3)

Definition

Copy

    function block_roblox_window(state: boolean): ()

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#parameters-2)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

state

boolean

Whether or not you're trying to block or unblock the window.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-3)

Description

Will effectively disable input pass-through on the overlay, forcing you to interact with **it** rather than the game. This is useful when creating custom a user-interface.

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#pointer_to_userdata)

pointer\_to\_userdata


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition-4)

Definition

Copy

    function pointer_to_userdata(address: number): userdata

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#parameters-3)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

address

number

The address that you want to turn into a userdata.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#returns-1)

Returns

Copy

    userdata

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-4)

Description

This is a useful function that you'll find yourself utilizing when interacting with the memory functions. This will effectively turn valid addresses back into **wolurld objects**, allowing you to index/namecall them.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#code-samples-2)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Find the DataModel by reading Workspace's parent offset, and then recasting it back to userdata.
    local Parent = memory.readu64(workspace, 0x50)
    local DataModel = pointer_to_userdata(Parent)
    
    print(DataModel == game) -- Ideally, would be true, however due to version changes, 0x50 might be an invalid offset.

* * *

Description

Returns the number amount of **FPS** (frames per second) that the overlay is currently running at.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#add_model_data)

add\_model\_data


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition-9)

Definition

Copy

    function add_model_data(data: table, key: string): boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#parameters-4)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

data

table

Character data structure with fields like `Username` (string), `Displayname` (string), `Userid` (number), `Character` (Instance), `PrimaryPart` (Instance), `Head` (Instance), `LeftLeg` (Instance), `LeftArm` (Instance), `RightLeg` (Instance), `RightArm` (Instance), `Torso` (Instance), `ToolName` (string), `TeamName` (string), `BodyHeightScale` (number), `RigType` (number), `Whitelisted` (boolean), `Archenemies` (boolean), `Aimbot_Part` (Instance), `Aimbot_TP_Part` (Instance), `Triggerbot_Part` (Instance), `Health` (number), `MaxHealth` (number), `body_parts_data` (table), `full_body_data` (table).

key

string

Unique identifier for storing the model data.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#returns-6)

Returns

Copy

    boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-9)

Description

Declares a new character model data under the given key for use in targeting and ESP. Processed in a dedicated model thread, and will return `true` on success.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#code-samples-3)

Code Samples

Copy

    local data = {
        Username = "Player1",
        Displayname = "CoolPlayer",
        Userid = 123456,
        Character = workspace.Player1.Character,
        PrimaryPart = workspace.Player1.Character.HumanoidRootPart,
        -- ... other fields
    }
    add_model_data(data, "player1_key")

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#edit_model_data)

edit\_model\_data


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition-10)

Definition

Copy

    function edit_model_data(data: table, key: string): boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#parameters-5)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

data

table

Partial updates with fields like `RigType` (number), `Whitelisted` (boolean), `Archenemies` (boolean), `Aimbot_Part` (Instance), `Aimbot_TP_Part` (Instance), `Triggerbot_Part` (Instance), `Health` (number), `MaxHealth` (number), `BodyHeightScale` (number).

key

string

Key of existing model data to update.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#returns-7)

Returns

Copy

    boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-10)

Description

Updates specific fields in existing model data stored under the key. Efficient for runtime changes like health or target parts. Returns `true` on success.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#code-samples-4)

Code Samples

Copy

    local edit = {
        Health = 50,
        Aimbot_Part = workspace.Player1.Character.Head
    }
    edit_model_data(edit, "player1_key")

* * *

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#override_local_data)

override\_local\_data


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition-13)

Definition

Copy

    function override_local_data(data: table): boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#parameters-7)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

data

table

Local player data with fields like `LocalPlayer` (userdata), `Displayname` (string), `Username` (string), `Userid` (number), `Character` (userdata), `Team` (userdata), `RootPart` (userdata), `LeftFoot` (userdata), `Head` (userdata), `LowerTorso` (userdata), `Tool` (userdata), `Humanoid` (userdata), `Health` (number), `MaxHealth` (number), `RigType` (number).

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#returns-10)

Returns

Copy

    boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-13)

Description

Sets or overrides local player data for UI rendering and local thread processing. Returns `true` on success.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#code-samples-5)

Code Samples

Copy

    local data = {
        LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer,
        Character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character,
        -- ... other fields
    }
    override_local_data(data)

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#clear_local_data)

clear\_local\_data


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#definition-14)

Definition

Copy

    function clear_local_data(): boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#returns-11)

Returns

Copy

    boolean

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/miscellaneous#description-14)

Description

Clears all local player data. Returns `true` on success.

# Input | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/input.md)

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/input#keypress)

keypress


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/input#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function keypress(keycode: number): ()

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/input#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

keycode

number

Virtual keycode to press

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/input#description)

Description

Simulates a key press for the given virtual keycode.

> **Note:** Virtual key codes: [Microsoft Docs](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/desktop/inputdev/virtual-key-codes)

* * *

# File System | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#dofile)

dofile


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function dofile(path: string): (... any)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#returns)

Returns

Copy

    (... any)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#description)

Description

Effectively `loadstring(readfile(path))()`. Loads and executes a luau file, returning any values the file returns.

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#loadfile)

loadfile


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#definition-1)

Definition

Copy

    function loadfile(path: string): (... any)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#returns-1)

Returns

Copy

    (... any)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#description-1)

Description

Loads a luau file and returns it as a function. Call the returned function to execute the file's code.

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#writefile)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/core/file-system#description-2)

# Vector3 | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3.md)
.

A 3D vector with X, Y, and Z components.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#constructors)

Constructors


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#vector3.new)

Vector3.new

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function Vector3.new(x: number, y: number, z: number): Vector3
    function Vector3.new(): Vector3

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

x

number

The X component

y

number

The Y component

z

number

The Z component

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#returns)

Returns

Type

Vector3

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#description)

Description

Creates a new Vector3. If no parameters are provided, creates a zero vector (0, 0, 0).

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Create a vector
    local vec = Vector3.new(10, 20, 30)
    
    -- Zero vector
    local zero = Vector3.new()
    print(zero) -- Vector3(0, 0, 0)
    
    -- Unit vectors
    local right = Vector3.new(1, 0, 0)
    local up = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
    local forward = Vector3.new(0, 0, 1)

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#properties)

Properties


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#x)

Copy

    Vector3.X: number

The X component of the vector.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#y)

Y

Copy

    Vector3.Y: number

The Y component of the vector.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#z)

Z

Copy

    Vector3.Z: number

The Z component of the vector.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#magnitude)

Magnitude

Copy

    Vector3.Magnitude: number

The length of the vector.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#unit)

Unit

Copy

    Vector3.Unit: Vector3

A normalized version of the vector (length of 1).

* * *

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#lerp)

Lerp

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#definition-3)

Definition

Copy

    function Vector3:Lerp(goal: Vector3, alpha: number): Vector3

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#parameters-3)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

goal

Vector3

The target vector to interpolate towards

alpha

number

The interpolation factor (0 to 1)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#returns-3)

Returns

Type

Vector3

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#description-3)

Description

Returns a Vector3 interpolated between this vector and the goal vector by the alpha amount.

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#metatables)

Metatables


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#add)

\_\_add

Adds two vectors.

Copy

    local v1 = Vector3.new(1, 2, 3)
    local v2 = Vector3.new(4, 5, 6)
    local result = v1 + v2 -- Vector3(5, 7, 9)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#sub)

\_\_sub

Subtracts one vector from another.

Copy

    local v1 = Vector3.new(5, 7, 9)
    local v2 = Vector3.new(1, 2, 3)
    local result = v1 - v2 -- Vector3(4, 5, 6)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#mul)

\_\_mul

Multiplies a vector by a scalar or another vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector3.new(1, 2, 3)
    local scaled = vec * 2 -- Vector3(2, 4, 6)
    
    -- Component-wise multiplication
    local v1 = Vector3.new(2, 3, 4)
    local v2 = Vector3.new(1, 2, 3)
    local result = v1 * v2 -- Vector3(2, 6, 12)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#div)

\_\_div

Divides a vector by a scalar or another vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector3.new(10, 20, 30)
    local scaled = vec / 2 -- Vector3(5, 10, 15)
    
    -- Component-wise division
    local v1 = Vector3.new(10, 20, 30)
    local v2 = Vector3.new(2, 4, 5)
    local result = v1 / v2 -- Vector3(5, 5, 6)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#unm)

\_\_unm

Negates a vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector3.new(1, 2, 3)
    local negated = -vec -- Vector3(-1, -2, -3)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#eq)

\_\_eq

Compares two vectors for equality.

Copy

    local v1 = Vector3.new(1, 2, 3)
    local v2 = Vector3.new(1, 2, 3)
    local v3 = Vector3.new(4, 5, 6)
    
    print(v1 == v2) -- true
    print(v1 == v3) -- false

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector3#tostring)

\_\_tostring

Returns a string representation of the vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector3.new(10, 20, 30)
    print(vec) -- "Vector3(10, 20, 30)"

[PreviousClasses](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes)
[NextColor3](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Color3 | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3.md)
.

A data type representing a color with red, green, and blue components.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#constructors)

Constructors


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#color3.new)

Color3.new

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function Color3.new(r: number, g: number, b: number): Color3

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

r

number

Red component (0 to 1)

g

number

Green component (0 to 1)

b

number

Blue component (0 to 1)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#returns)

Returns

Type

Color3

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#description)

Description

Creates a new Color3 from RGB values in the range 0 to 1.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Pure red
    local red = Color3.new(1, 0, 0)
    
    -- Pure green
    local green = Color3.new(0, 1, 0)
    
    -- Pure blue
    local blue = Color3.new(0, 0, 1)
    
    -- White
    local white = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
    
    -- Gray (50%)
    local gray = Color3.new(0.5, 0.5, 0.5)

* * *

    -- Pure blue (hue = 2/3)
    local blue = Color3.fromHSV(2/3, 1, 1)
    
    -- Desaturated red (pink)
    local pink = Color3.fromHSV(0, 0.5, 1)

Metatables

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#index)

    local g = color.G -- 0.502
    local b = color.B -- 0.251

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3#eq)

\_\_eq

Compares two Color3 values for equality.

Copy

    local color1 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    local color2 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    local color3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
    
    print(color1 == color2) -- true
    print(color1 == color3) -- false

# Vector2 | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2.md)
.

A 2D vector with X and Y components.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#constructors)

Constructors


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#vector2.new)

Vector2.new

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function Vector2.new(x: number, y: number): Vector2
    function Vector2.new(): Vector2

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

x

number

The X component

y

number

The Y component

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#returns)

Returns

Type

Vector2

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#description)

Description

Creates a new Vector2. If no parameters are provided, creates a zero vector (0, 0).

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Create a vector
    local vec = Vector2.new(100, 200)
    
    -- Zero vector
    local zero = Vector2.new()
    print(zero) -- Vector2(0, 0)
    
    -- Unit vectors
    local right = Vector2.new(1, 0)
    local up = Vector2.new(0, 1)

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#properties)

A normalized version of the vector (length of 1).

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#metatables)

Metatables


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#add)

\_\_add

Adds two vectors.

Copy

    local v1 = Vector2.new(10, 20)
    local v2 = Vector2.new(5, 15)
    local result = v1 + v2 -- Vector2(15, 35)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#sub)

\_\_sub

Subtracts one vector from another.

Copy

    local v1 = Vector2.new(10, 20)
    local v2 = Vector2.new(5, 15)
    local result = v1 - v2 -- Vector2(5, 5)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#mul)

\_\_mul

Multiplies a vector by a scalar or another vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector2.new(10, 20)
    local scaled = vec * 2 -- Vector2(20, 40)
    
    -- Component-wise multiplication
    local v1 = Vector2.new(2, 3)
    local v2 = Vector2.new(4, 5)
    local result = v1 * v2 -- Vector2(8, 15)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#div)

\_\_div

Divides a vector by a scalar or another vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector2.new(100, 200)
    local scaled = vec / 2 -- Vector2(50, 100)
    
    -- Component-wise division
    local v1 = Vector2.new(100, 200)
    local v2 = Vector2.new(10, 20)
    local result = v1 / v2 -- Vector2(10, 10)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#unm)

\_\_unm

Negates a vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector2.new(10, 20)
    local negated = -vec -- Vector2(-10, -20)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#eq)

\_\_eq

Compares two vectors for equality.

Copy

    local v1 = Vector2.new(10, 20)
    local v2 = Vector2.new(10, 20)
    local v3 = Vector2.new(5, 15)
    
    print(v1 == v2) -- true
    print(v1 == v3) -- false

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/vector2#tostring)

\_\_tostring

Returns a string representation of the vector.

Copy

    local vec = Vector2.new(100, 200)
    print(vec) -- "Vector2(100, 200)"

[NextLibraries](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries)

# luau | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#compile)

compile


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function luau.compile(source: string, options: {
        optimizationLevel: 0 | 1 | 2?,
        coverageLevel: 0 | 1 | 2?,
        debugLevel: 0 | 1 | 2?
    }): string

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

source

string

The Luau source code to compile.

options

table

Compilation settings (optimization, coverage, debug).

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#description)

Description

Compiles the given source code into Luau bytecode. An error will be thrown if the source code contains syntax errors or other issues that prevent successful compilation.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    local bytecode = luau.compile("print('Hello, World!')", {
        optimizationLevel = 2,
        coverageLevel = 0,
        debugLevel = 1,
    })
    
    local func = load(bytecode)
    func()  -- Outputs: Hello, World!

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#load)

load


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#definition-1)

Definition

Copy

    function luau.load(bytecode: string, options: {
        debugName: string?,
        environment: { [string]: any }?,
        injectGlobals: boolean?,
        codegenEnabled: boolean?
    }): (... any?) -> (... any?)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#parameters-1)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

bytecode

string

Compiled Luau bytecode.

options

table

Loading options (debug name, environment, codegen).

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#description-1)

Description

Loads a function from the given Luau bytecode string. An error will be thrown if the bytecode is invalid or cannot be loaded. Note that if `environment` is enabled, native code generation and optimizations are forcefully disabled.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/luau#code-samples-1)

Code Samples

Copy

    local bytecode = luau.compile("return 42", {
        optimizationLevel = 2,
        coverageLevel = 0,
        debugLevel = 1,
    })
    
    local func = luau.load(bytecode, "MyChunk")
    print(func())  -- Outputs: 42

[Previouscrypt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/crypt)
[Nextmemory](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory)

Last updated 4 months ago

# memory | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#types)

Types


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Description

Range / Format

**i8**

Signed 8-bit

\[-128, 127\]

**u8**

Unsigned 8-bit

\[0, 255\]

**i16**

Signed 16-bit

\[-32,768, 32,767\]

**u16**

Unsigned 16-bit

\[0, 65,535\]

**i32**

Signed 32-bit

\[-2.1B, 2.1B\]

**u32**

Unsigned 32-bit

\[0, 4.2B\]

**i64**

Signed 64-bit

Approximate (Casted to Double)

**u64**

Unsigned 64-bit

Approximate (Casted to Double)

**f32**

32-bit Float

IEEE 754 Single

**f64**

64-bit Float

IEEE 754 Double

> **Note:** Luau does not natively support 64-bit integers. As a result, **i64** and **u64** operations are **approximations**; these values are cast to a double-precision float, which may lead to precision loss or rounding for extremely large integers.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#functions)

Functions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#read-type)

read\[type\]

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function memory.read[type](address: number): number
    function memory.read[type](source: userdata, offset: number): number

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#description)

Description

Reads data of a specific type from a raw memory address or an offset from a `userdata`. Note that \[type\] has to be replaced with a valid type that can be found above. Valid example is: `memory.readu32(workspace, 0x50)`.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#memory.write-type)

memory.write\[type\]

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#definition-1)

Definition

Copy

    function memory.write[type](address: number, value: number): ()
    function memory.write[type](destination: userdata, offset: number, value: number): ()

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#description-1)

Description

Writes a value of a specific type to a memory address or `userdata` offset. Note that \[type\] has to be replaced with a valid type that can be found above. Valid example is: `memory.writeu32(workspace, 0x50)`.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#memory.readbits)

memory.readbits

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#definition-2)

Definition

Copy

    function memory.readbits(address: number, bitOffset: number, bitSize: number): number
    function memory.readbits(source: userdata, offset: number, bitOffset: number, bitSize: number): number

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#description-2)

Description

Reads a range of bits (up to 32) from the target, starting at `bitOffset`.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#memory.writebits)

memory.writebits

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#definition-3)

Definition

Copy

    function memory.writebits(address: number, bitOffset: number, bitSize: number, value: number): ()
    function memory.writebits(destination: userdata, offset: number, bitOffset: number, bitSize: number, value: number): ()

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#description-3)

Description

Writes a range of bits (up to 32) from `value` to the destination at `bitOffset`.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#memory.readstring)

memory.readstring

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#definition-4)

Definition

Copy

    function memory.readstring(address: number): string
    function memory.readstring(source: userdata, offset: number): string

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#description-4)

Description

Reads a raw null-terminated string or byte sequence from the target location.

* * *

###

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#definition-11)

Definition

Copy

    function memory.changed(address: number, type: string, callback: (self: userdata, new: any, old: any) -> (), iterations: number?): userdata
    function memory.changed(source: userdata, offset: number, type: string, callback: (self: userdata, new: any, old: any) -> (), iterations: number?): userdata

#### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory#description-11)

Description

Establishes a listener on a memory location that triggers the `callback` whenever the value changes. Available types: `i8`, `u8`, `i16`, `u16`, `i32`, `u32`, `i64`, `u64`, `f32`, `f64`, `string`.

# Drawing | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Drawing itself, within **Severe** refers to a library which has functions for static ([retained](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Retained_mode)
) rendering of objects. We offer 3 different ways of rendering:

*   **Dynamic:** Offering best performance, and fast usage.
    
*   **Immediate:** Ideal for a small amount of objects, or if the objects move.
    
*   **Static:** [Retained](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Retained_mode)
     drawing, being best if you can manage it properly, or for user interfaces.
    

[Previoustask](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task)
[NextClasses](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/classes)

Last updated 4 months ago

---

# WebsocketClient | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient.md)
.

A websocket client for establishing and managing WebSocket connections.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#constructors)

Constructors


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#websocketclient.new)

WebsocketClient.new

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function WebsocketClient.new(url: string): WebsocketClient

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

url

string

The WebSocket connection URL

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#returns)

Returns

Type

WebsocketClient

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#description)

Description

Creates a new WebsocketClient and connects to the specified URL.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Create a WebSocket connection
    local ws = WebsocketClient.new("ws://example.com:8080")
    
    -- Handle incoming messages
    ws.DataReceived:Connect(function(payload, isBinary)
        if isBinary then
            print("Received binary data:", #payload, "bytes")
        else
            print("Received text:", payload)
        end
    end)
    
    -- Send a message
    ws:Send("Hello, server!")
    
    -- Disconnect when done
    ws:Disconnect()

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#properties)

Properties


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#url)

Url

Copy

    WebsocketClient.Url: string [readonly]

The WebSocket connection URL that this client is connected to. This property is read-only.

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#methods)

Methods


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#disconnect)

Disconnect

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#definition-1)

Definition

Copy

    function WebsocketClient:Disconnect(): ()

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#description-1)

Description

Disconnects the WebSocket. Yields until the client is fully disconnected. After calling this method, the WebSocket connection is closed and no further messages can be sent or received.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#code-samples-1)

Code Samples

Copy

    local ws = WebsocketClient.new("ws://example.com:8080")
    
    -- Do some work...
    ws:Send("Goodbye")
    
    -- Disconnect (yields until fully disconnected)
    ws:Disconnect()
    print("WebSocket disconnected")

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#send)

Send

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#definition-2)

Definition

Copy

    function WebsocketClient:Send(message: string, isBinary: boolean?): ()

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#parameters-1)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

message

string

The message payload to send

isBinary

boolean?

Whether to send as binary data (defaults to false)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#description-2)

Description

Sends a message through the WebSocket connection. The message can be sent as either text or binary data based on the `isBinary` parameter.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#code-samples-2)

Code Samples

Copy

    local ws = WebsocketClient.new("ws://example.com:8080")
    
    -- Send text message (default)
    ws:Send("Hello, world!")
    
    -- Explicitly send text
    ws:Send("Text message", false)
    
    -- Send binary data
    local binaryData = "\x01\x02\x03\x04"
    ws:Send(binaryData, true)

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#events)

Events


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#datareceived)

DataReceived

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#definition-3)

Definition

Copy

    WebsocketClient.DataReceived: Signal<(payload: string, isBinary: boolean) -> ()>

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#parameters-2)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

payload

string

The received message data

isBinary

boolean

Whether the received data is binary

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#description-3)

Description

Fires when data is received from the WebSocket connection. The event provides the payload as a string and a boolean indicating whether it's binary data.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/websocketclient#code-samples-3)

Code Samples

Copy

    local ws = WebsocketClient.new("ws://example.com:8080")
    
    -- Connect to the DataReceived event
    ws.DataReceived:Connect(function(payload, isBinary)
        if isBinary then
            print("Received binary payload of length:", #payload)
            -- Process binary data...
        else
            print("Received text message:", payload)
            -- Process text data...
        end
    end)
    
    -- Example with JSON parsing
    ws.DataReceived:Connect(function(payload, isBinary)
        if not isBinary then
            local success, data = pcall(function()
                return game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(payload)
            end)
            
            if success then
                print("Received JSON data:", data)
            else
                print("Received non-JSON text:", payload)
            end
        end
    end)

[PreviousColor3](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/color3)
[NextSignal](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/signal)

Last updated 4 months ago

# CFrame | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe.md)
.

A coordinate frame representing position and rotation in 3D space.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#constructors)

Constructors


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#cframe.new)

CFrame.new

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function CFrame.new(): CFrame
    function CFrame.new(x: number, y: number, z: number): CFrame
    function CFrame.new(position: Vector3): CFrame
    function CFrame.new(position: Vector3, lookAt: Vector3): CFrame
    function CFrame.new(x: number, y: number, z: number, qx: number, qy: number, qz: number, qw: number): CFrame
    function CFrame.new(x: number, y: number, z: number, R00: number, R01: number, R02: number, R10: number, R11: number, R12: number, R20: number, R21: number, R22: number): CFrame

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#description)

Description

Creates a new CFrame. Can be constructed in several ways:

*   Empty constructor creates an identity CFrame at (0, 0, 0)
    
*   Position-only creates a CFrame at the specified position with no rotation
    
*   Position and lookAt creates a CFrame positioned at the first argument, looking at the second
    
*   Position with quaternion values for rotation
    
*   Position with full rotation matrix components
    

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Identity CFrame
    local cf1 = CFrame.new()
    
    -- Position only
    local cf2 = CFrame.new(10, 20, 30)
    
    -- Position from Vector3
    local cf3 = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(5, 10, 15))
    
    -- Position looking at another position
    local cf4 = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0, 5, 0), Vector3.new(10, 5, 10))

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#cframe.fromeuleranglesxyz)

CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#definition-1)

Definition

    function CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(rotation: Vector3): CFrame

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#parameters)

Description

Returns

Type

CFrame

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#description-1)

Description

Creates a rotated CFrame using Euler angles in X, Y, Z order (roll, pitch, yaw).

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#code-samples-1)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Rotate 90 degrees (π/2 radians) around Y-axis
    local cf = CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(0, math.pi/2, 0)
    
    -- Using Vector3
    local rotation = Vector3.new(0, math.pi/2, 0)
    local cf2 = CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(rotation)

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#methods)

Methods


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#inverse)

Inverse

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#definition-8)

Definition

Copy

    function CFrame:Inverse(): CFrame

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#returns-7)

Returns

Type

CFrame

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#description-8)

Description

Returns the inverse of this CFrame. When multiplied with the original, produces an identity CFrame.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#code-samples-4)

Code Samples

Copy

    local cf = CFrame.new(10, 20, 30)
    local inverse = cf:Inverse()
    local identity = cf * inverse -- Results in CFrame at origin

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#lerp)

Lerp

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#definition-9)

Definition

Copy

    function CFrame:Lerp(goal: CFrame, alpha: number): CFrame

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#parameters-7)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

goal

CFrame

The target CFrame to interpolate towards

alpha

number

The interpolation factor (0 to 1)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#returns-8)

Returns

Type

CFrame

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#description-9)

Description

Returns a CFrame interpolated between this CFrame and the goal CFrame by the alpha amount.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#code-samples-5)

Code Samples

Copy

    local start = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
    local goal = CFrame.new(10, 10, 10)
    local halfway = start:Lerp(goal, 0.5) -- CFrame at (5, 5, 5)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#toobjectspace)

ToObjectSpace

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#definition-11)

    function CFrame:ToObjectSpace(cf: CFrame): CFrame

Metatables


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#index)

\_\_index

Allows property access on CFrame values.

Copy

    local cf = CFrame.new(10, 20, 30)
    local pos = cf.Position -- Vector3(10, 20, 30)
    local rightVector = cf.RightVector
    local upVector = cf.UpVector
    local lookVector = cf.LookVector

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#mul)

\_\_mul

Multiplies two CFrames or transforms a Vector3.

Copy

    -- CFrame multiplication
    local cf1 = CFrame.new(10, 0, 0)
    local cf2 = CFrame.new(5, 0, 0)
    local result = cf1 * cf2 -- CFrame at (15, 0, 0)
    
    -- Transform a Vector3
    local cf = CFrame.new(10, 20, 30)
    local point = Vector3.new(1, 1, 1)
    local transformed = cf * point

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#add)

\_\_add

Translates a CFrame by a Vector3.

Copy

    local cf = CFrame.new(10, 20, 30)
    local offset = Vector3.new(5, 5, 5)
    local result = cf + offset -- CFrame at (15, 25, 35)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#sub)

\_\_sub

Translates a CFrame by the negative of a Vector3.

Copy

    local cf = CFrame.new(10, 20, 30)
    local offset = Vector3.new(5, 5, 5)
    local result = cf - offset -- CFrame at (5, 15, 25)

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/classes/cframe#tostring)

\_\_tostring

    local cf = CFrame.new(10, 20, 30)
    print(cf) -- "CFrame(10, 20, 30, 1, 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 1)"

# task | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task.md)
.

Task scheduler library providing thread management functions for asynchronous execution.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#functions)

Functions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#task.spawn)

task.spawn


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function task.spawn(functionOrThread: (() -> ()) | thread, ...: any): thread

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

functionOrThread

(() -> ()) | thread

The function or thread to execute immediately

...

any

Optional arguments to pass to the function

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#returns)

Returns

Type

thread

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#description)

Description

Immediately executes the provided function or resumes the provided thread in a separate thread without yielding the current thread. The new thread runs in parallel with the calling thread. Returns the thread that was spawned.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#code-samples)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Spawn a function
    task.spawn(function()
        print("This runs immediately in a new thread")
        task.wait(1)
        print("After 1 second")
    end)
    
    -- Spawn with arguments
    task.spawn(function(message, delay)
        task.wait(delay)
        print(message)
    end, "Hello!", 2)
    
    -- Spawn a thread
    local thread = coroutine.create(function()
        print("Thread spawned")
    end)
    task.spawn(thread)

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#task.defer)

task.defer


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#definition-1)

Definition

Copy

    function task.defer(functionOrThread: (() -> ()) | thread, ...: any): thread

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#parameters-1)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

functionOrThread

(() -> ()) | thread

The function or thread to execute after deferral

...

any

Optional arguments to pass to the function

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#returns-1)

Returns

Type

thread

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#description-1)

Description

Defers the execution of the provided function or thread until the next resumption cycle. Unlike `task.spawn`, deferred functions do not run immediately but wait until the current thread yields. This is useful for scheduling work that should happen after the current frame or operation completes.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#code-samples-1)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Defer a function
    task.defer(function()
        print("This runs after the current thread yields")
    end)
    
    -- Defer with arguments
    task.defer(function(text)
        print("Deferred: " .. text)
    end, "Hello, world!")
    
    print("This prints first")
    
    -- Output:
    -- This prints first
    -- This runs after the current thread yields
    -- Deferred: Hello, world!

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#task.cancel)

task.cancel


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#definition-2)

Definition

Copy

    function task.cancel(thread: thread): ()

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#parameters-2)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

thread

thread

The thread to cancel

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#description-2)

Description

Cancels a thread that was created with `task.spawn`, `task.defer`, or `task.delay`. Once cancelled, the thread will not resume execution. If the thread is already completed or cancelled, this function has no effect.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#code-samples-2)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Cancel a spawned thread
    local thread = task.spawn(function()
        task.wait(5)
        print("This will never print")
    end)
    
    task.wait(1)
    task.cancel(thread)
    print("Thread cancelled")
    
    -- Cancel a deferred thread
    local deferredThread = task.defer(function()
        print("This will not execute")
    end)
    task.cancel(deferredThread)

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#task.delay)

task.delay


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#definition-3)

Definition

Copy

    function task.delay(duration: number, functionOrThread: (() -> ()) | thread, ...: any): thread

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#parameters-3)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

duration

number

The time in seconds to wait before execution

functionOrThread

(() -> ()) | thread

The function or thread to execute after delay

...

any

Optional arguments to pass to the function

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#returns-2)

Returns

Type

thread

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#description-3)

Description

Schedules a function or thread to execute after the specified duration in seconds. The function runs in a separate thread after the delay. Returns the thread that will be executed. This is useful for scheduling delayed operations without blocking the current thread.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#code-samples-3)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Delay execution by 3 seconds
    task.delay(3, function()
        print("This prints after 3 seconds")
    end)
    
    -- Delay with arguments
    task.delay(5, function(message, count)
        for i = 1, count do
            print(message)
        end
    end, "Delayed message", 3)
    
    -- Delay a thread
    local thread = coroutine.create(function()
        print("Thread executed after delay")
    end)
    task.delay(2, thread)
    
    -- Cancel a delayed task
    local delayedThread = task.delay(10, function()
        print("This will be cancelled")
    end)
    task.wait(1)
    task.cancel(delayedThread)
    print("Delayed task cancelled")

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#task.wait)

task.wait


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#definition-4)

Definition

Copy

    function task.wait(duration: number?): number

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#parameters-4)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

duration

number?

The time in seconds to wait. Defaults to 0 if not provided.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#returns-3)

Returns

Type

number

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#description-4)

Description

Yields the current thread for at least the specified duration in seconds. Returns the actual time elapsed. This is the preferred way to yield execution in modern Luau code, replacing the legacy `wait()` function.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/task#code-samples-4)

Code Samples

Copy

    -- Wait for 2 seconds
    local elapsed = task.wait(2)
    print("Waited for " .. elapsed .. " seconds")
    
    -- Wait with default duration
    task.wait() -- Waits for the next frame/cycle
    
    -- Use in a loop
    for i = 1, 5 do
        print("Iteration " .. i)
        task.wait(1)
    end
    
    -- Countdown timer
    for i = 10, 1, -1 do
        print(i)
        task.wait(1)
    end
    print("Blast off!")

[Previousmemory](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/libraries/memory)
[NextDrawing](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Static | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/static.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/static#functions)

Functions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/static#drawing.new)

Drawing.new

**Definition**

Copy

    function Drawing.new(class: string): userdata

**Parameters**

Name

Type

Description

class

string

Valid classes can be found under the "Classes" sub-folder.

**Description**

Will create a new static drawing on the screen, it's retained, meaning you will have to manually describe it (set it's color, position, size), and manually clean-up.

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/static#drawing.clear)

Drawing.clear

**Definition**

Copy

    function Drawing.clear(): ()

**Description**

Will clear all the static objects created, this will also include static objects that were created by other scripts.

* * *

> **Note:** Not removing static drawings can result in degraded performance and memory leaks. Creating a lot of static drawings may result in render thread error, this is a known issue.

[PreviousImmediate](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/immediate)
[NextWorld](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Dynamic | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Dynamic drawing allows you to automatically attach drawing objects to 3D world positions or instances. Drawing objects automatically update their screen position based on the camera's view of the linked points.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic#functions)

Functions


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic#drawing.attach)

Drawing.attach

**Definition**

Copy

    function Drawing.attach(config: { [Drawing]: AttachmentConfig }): Cluster

**Parameters**

Name

Type

Description

config

{ \[Drawing\]: AttachmentConfig }

A table mapping drawing objects to their attachment configurations

**Returns**

Type

Description

Cluster

A cluster object that can be destroyed, paused, or resumed

**Description**

Attaches drawing objects to 3D points in the world. The drawing objects will automatically update their screen positions based on the camera's view of the linked points. Each drawing object can be configured with different attachment properties depending on its type.

**Attachment Configurations**

For `Square`, `Circle`, `Text`, `Image`:

Property

Type

Description

Link

Point

The point to attach the drawing to

Size

UDim2

Size of the drawing (Scale/Offset)

AnchorPoint

Vector2

Anchor point for positioning (0-1 range)

For `Line`:

Property

Type

Description

From

Point

Starting point of the line

To

Point

Ending point of the line

**Code Samples**

Copy

    local Head = PointInstance.new(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head :: BasePart)
    local Mesh = PointInstance.new(workspace.SpawnLocation :: BasePart)
    
    local Square = Drawing.new 'Square'
    Square.Visible = true
    Square.Filled = true
    Square.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 125)
    
    local Line = Drawing.new 'Line'
    Line.Visible = true
    Line.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    Line.Thickness = 2
    
    local Cluster = Drawing.attach {
        [Square] = {
            Link = Head,
            Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 1),
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
        },
    
        [Line] = {
            From = Head,
            To = Mesh,
        }
    }
    
    task.wait(10)
    
    -- Later, when done:
    Cluster:Destroy()

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic#classes)

Classes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic#pointinstance)

PointInstance

**Definition**

Copy

    PointInstance.new(instance: BasePart): PointInstance

**Description**

Creates a point tracker for an instance with a CFrame property. The point automatically tracks the instance's position in the world. Only instances that have a CFrame property (e.g., BasePart) can be used.

**Properties**

Property

Type

Description

CFrame

CFrame

The current CFrame of the tracked instance

Size

Vector3

The current Size of the tracked instance

Active

boolean

Whether the point is actively tracking the instance

**Methods**

Method

Description

Destroy

Stops tracking and cleans up resources

**Code Samples**

Copy

    local Head = PointInstance.new(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head :: BasePart)
    
    -- Access properties
    print(Head.CFrame)
    print(Head.Size)
    print(Head.Active)
    
    task.wait(10)
    
    -- Clean up:
    Head:Destroy()

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic#point3d)

Point3D

**Definition**

Copy

    Point3D.new(position: Vector3): Point3D

**Description**

Creates a point at a fixed world-space position. The point represents a static location in 3D space.

**Properties**

Property

Type

Description

Position

Vector3

The world-space position of the point

Active

boolean

Whether the point is active

**Methods**

Method

Description

Destroy

Cleans up the point and its resources

**Code Samples**

Copy

    local StaticPoint = Point3D.new(Vector3.new(0, 10, 0))
    
    -- Access properties
    print(StaticPoint.Position)
    print(StaticPoint.Active)
    
    -- Clean up when done
    StaticPoint:Destroy()

* * *

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/dynamic#cluster)

Cluster

**Description**

A cluster is returned by `Drawing.attach` and manages a group of attached drawing objects. It provides methods to control the lifecycle of all attached drawings.

**Methods**

Method

Description

Destroy

Destroys the cluster and all attached drawing objects

Pause

Pauses automatic updates for all drawings in the cluster

Resume

Resumes automatic updates for all drawings in the cluster

**Code Samples**

Copy

    local Head = PointInstance.new(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head :: BasePart)
    
    local Square = Drawing.new 'Square'
    Square.Visible = true
    
    local Cluster = Drawing.attach {
        [Square] = {
            Link = Head,
            Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 1),
            AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
        }
    }
    
    -- Pause updates
    Cluster:Pause()
    
    -- Resume updates
    Cluster:Resume()
    
    -- Clean up everything
    Cluster:Destroy()

[PreviousTriangle](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/classes/triangle)
[NextImmediate](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/immediate)

# Immediate | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/immediate.md)
.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/immediate#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Traditional drawing uses **retained mode**—objects persist until removed. **DrawingImmediate** is **immediate mode**; objects exist only during `RunService.Render` calls.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/immediate#examples)

Examples


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    local Players = game:GetService("Players")
    local CurrentCamera = workspace.CurrentCamera
    local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
    
    RunService.Render:Connect(function()
        for Index, Player in Players:GetChildren() do
            local Character = Player.Character
            if not Character then continue end
            
            local Head = Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
            if not Head then continue end
            
            local Screen, Visible = CurrentCamera:WorldToScreenPoint(Head.Position)
            
            if Visible then
                DrawingImmediate.OutlinedText(Screen, 14, Color3.fromRGB(125, 165, 255), 1, Player.Name, true, "Tamzen")
            end
        end
    end)

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/immediate#functions)

Functions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Call inside `RunService.Render` to avoid flickering. No return values.

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/drawing/immediate#line)

# DataModel | v-severe

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel.md)
.

The DataModel (accessed via the `game` global) is the root object of the game hierarchy.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#httpget)

HttpGet


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#definition)

Definition

Copy

    function game:HttpGet(url: string): string

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

url

string

The URL to send a GET request to

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#returns)

Returns

Type

string

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#description)

Description

Sends an HTTP GET request to the specified URL and returns the response as a string.

* * *

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#httppost)

HttpPost


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#definition-1)

Definition

Copy

    function game:HttpPost(url: string, data: string): string

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#parameters-1)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

url

string

The URL to send a POST request to

data

string

The data to send in the POST request

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#returns-1)

Returns

Type

string

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/datamodel#description-1)

Description

Sends an HTTP POST request to the specified URL with the provided data and returns the response as a string.

* * *

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/model#definition)

Copy

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/model#description)

Description

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/readme.md).

# Landing

Welcome to \*\*Severe's user guide\*\*, within the articles, we cover user installation, usage, and reference to our implementation of the \*\*Luau\*\*.

## Product Description

\*\*Severe\*\* is an external, being one of the first on the market \*\*post-Hyperion\*\*, it is a very powerful and undetected tool on \*\*Roblox\*\*. It has a staggering, modern visuals, a flexible aimbot, and other useful tools, as well as most importantly, a \*\*Luau\*\* environment, allowing those familiar with the language to further tailor their experience.

## Tooling

Before proceeding further, if you're here for \*\*Luau\*\* development, please ensure proper tooling. We recommend:

\* \*\*Zed:\*\* as a code editor, it is open-source and is blazingly fast, offering alot of extensions and settings to tailor the UI, \*\*Visual Studio Code\*\* can also be used.
\* \*\*Figma:\*\* for any graphical work, for example making a UI, we recommend using this, as it is a straight-forward tool allowing you to sketch and convert UI for \*\*Severe\*\*.


---

## Querying This Documentation
If you need additional information that is not directly available in this page, you can query the documentation dynamically by asking a question.

Perform an HTTP GET request on the current page URL with the \`ask\` query parameter, and the optional \`goal\` query parameter:

\`\`\`
GET https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/introduction/readme.md?ask=<question>&goal=<endgoal>
\`\`\`

\`ask\` is the immediate question: it should be specific, self-contained, and written in natural language.
\`goal\` is optional and describes the broader end goal you are ultimately trying to accomplish on behalf of the user. GitBook uses it to tailor the answer towards what is most useful for that goal.

The response will contain a direct answer to the question and relevant excerpts and sources from the documentation.

Use this mechanism when the answer is not explicitly present in the current page, you need clarification or additional context, or you want to retrieve related documentation sections.

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/camera#worldtoscreenpoint)

WorldToScreenPoint


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/camera#definition-9)

Definition

Copy

    function Camera:WorldToScreenPoint(worldPosition: Vector3): (Vector3, boolean)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/camera#parameters)

Parameters

Name

Type

Description

worldPosition

Vector3

The position in world space

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/camera#returns)

Returns

Type

(Vector3, boolean)

### 

[](https://v-severe.gitbook.io/landing/reference/world/camera#description-9)

Description

Converts a world position to screen coordinates. Returns a Vector3 with X and Y as screen coordinates (Z is depth), and a boolean indicating if the point is visible on screen.
